That\n// reconciles state for the kubelet volume manager.\ntype Reconciler interface {\n\t// Starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically, checks\n\t// if volumes that should be attached are attached and volumes that should\n\t// be detached are detached. If during this time the volume\n// becomes used by a new pod, the detach request will be aborted and the timer\n// cleared.\nfunc NewReconciler(\n\tloopPeriod time.Duration,\n\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration time.Duration,\n\tsyncDuration time.Duration,\n\tdisableReconciliationSync bool,\n\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool,\n\tdesiredStateOfWorld cache.DesiredStateOfWorld,\n\tactualStateOfWorld cache.ActualStateOfWorld,\n\tattacherDetacher operationexecutor.OperationExecutor,\n\tnodeStatusUpdater statusupdater.NodeStatusUpdater,\n\tnodeLister corelisters.NodeLister,\n\trecorder record.EventRecorder) Reconciler {\n\treturn &reconciler{\n\t\tloopPeriod:                  loopPeriod,\n\t\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration:   maxWaitForUnmountDuration,\n\t\tsyncDuration:                syncDuration,\n\t\tdisableReconciliationSync:   disableReconciliationSync,\n\t\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout: disableForceDetachOnTimeout,\n\t\tdesiredStateOfWorld:         desiredStateOfWorld,\n\t\tactualStateOfWorld:          actualStateOfWorld,\n\t\tattacherDetacher:            attacherDetacher,\n\t\tnodeStatusUpdater:           nodeStatusUpdater,\n\t\tnodeLister:                  nodeLister,\n\t\ttimeOfLastSync:              time.Now(),\n\t\trecorder:                    recorder,\n\t}\n}\n\ntype reconciler struct {\n\tloopPeriod                  time.Duration\n\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration   time.Duration\n\tsyncDuration                time.Duration\n\tdesiredStateOfWorld         cache.DesiredStateOfWorld\n\tactualStateOfWorld          cache.ActualStateOfWorld","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":435}}}

The key pattern involves several components:\\n\\n1. **ControllerDescriptor Registration** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:495-522):\\n   Controllers are registered via `ControllerDescriptor` structs that contain a Name() and InitFunc(). The NewControllerDescriptors() function creates a map of all known controllers and their descriptors using a register() function. Each descriptor includes the controller's initialization function.\\n\\n2. **InitFunc Pattern** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:419):\\n   Each controller is defined by an `InitFunc` which is called to create and start the controller. The signature is:\\n   `type InitFunc func(ctx context.Context, controllerContext ControllerContext, controllerName string) (controller controller.Interface, enabled bool, err error)`\\n\\n3. **Controller Interface** (staging/src/k8s.io/controller-manager/controller/interfaces.go:26-29):\\n   Controllers must implement the `Interface` interface which requires a Name() method. Additional optional interfaces include Debuggable and HealthCheckable for debugging and health checks.\\n\\n4. **StartController Entry Point** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/controllermanager.go:710-761):\\n   The StartController() function orchestrates controller startup. It:\\n   - Validates feature gates\\n   - Calls the controller's InitFunc to create the controller\\n   - Registers debugging handlers if the controller implements Debuggable\\n   - Registers health checks if the controller implements HealthCheckable\\n\\n5. **Example: Deployment Controller Registration** (cmd/kube-controller-manager/app/apps.go:98-105):\\n   Controllers are registered with descriptors like:\\n   ```go\\n   func newDeploymentControllerDescriptor() *ControllerDescriptor {\\n       return &ControllerDescriptor{\\n           name:     names.DeploymentController,\\n           aliases:  []string{\\\"deployment\\\"},\\n           initFunc: startDeploymentController,\\n       }\\n   }\\n   ```\\n\\n6. **Initialization and Reconciliation Loop** (pkg/controller/deployment/deployment_controller.go:100-185):\\n   The startDeploymentController InitFunc creates a DeploymentController and calls its Run() method. The controller:\\n   - Sets up event handlers on informers (AddEventHandler) to watch Deployment, ReplicaSet, and Pod resources\\n   - Uses a work queue to queue items that need reconciliation\\n   - Spawns multiple worker goroutines that process items from the queue\\n   - Each worker calls syncDeployment (the syncHandler) to perform the actual reconciliation\\n\\n7. **Worker and Sync Pattern** (pkg/controller/deployment/deployment_controller.go:482-625):\\n   The worker() goroutine runs a reconciliation loop that:\\n   - Dequeues items from the work queue\\n   - Calls syncDeployment() to reconcile the deployment's desired state with the actual state\\n   - Handles retries and backoff using rate limiting\\n\\nThis pattern is the kubernetes equivalent of the controller-runtime's SetupWithManager approach. While controller-runtime uses a Reconciler interface with SetupWithManager() to register controllers, kubernetes controllers use ControllerDescriptor with InitFunc to register themselves with the manager.
